class="elementor-element elementor-element-27a00e7 e-flex e-con-boxed e-con e-parent" data-id="27a00e7" data-element_type="container" data-settings="{&quot;content_width&quot;:&quot;boxed&quot;}" data-core-v316-plus="true"> <div class="e-con-inner"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-1311c5c e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child" data-id="1311c5c" data-element_type="container" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h2 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Kingdom Of Learning</h2> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-d6736ba elementor-widget__width-initial elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="d6736ba" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container">  <p>Character development takes center stage in a child’s growth at My Little Kingdom</p> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-b131ec4 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor nitro-offscreen" data-id="b131ec4" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>My Little Kingdom stemmed from the vision of our Principal, Ms Yvonne Yeo. Her vision for good moral education helped to design the school’s methodology for an enriching preschool journey.&nbsp;</p><p>We believe that while academic success and being smart is important, inculcating good morals and the right values—things that will follow through to your child lives—are just as essential to their development.&nbsp;</p><p>At our preschool, the credo of ‘children come first’ is embraced. The uniqueness of every child is emphasised by creating a patient and nurturing environment that allows the child to feel at ease and cared for.</p> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-3c8fb41 e-con-full e-flex e-con e-child nitro-offscreen" data-id="3c8fb41" data-element_type="container" data-settings="{&quot;content_width&quot;:&quot;full&quot;}"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-66bbfc8 elementor-widget elementor-widget-image" data-id="66bbfc8" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="image.default"> <div nitro-lazy-src="https://cdn-lhcmd.nitrocdn.com/nUDVRQcwyFdFISPzifbloexvohdTucKY/assets/images/optimized/rev-7a18d84/www.mylittlekingdom.com.sg/wp-content/uploads/2023/11/Image-40.png" </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-028306c elementor-widget elementor-widget-heading" data-id="028306c" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="heading.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <h3 class="elementor-heading-title elementor-size-default">Yvonne Yeo</h3> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-fde3730 elementor-widget elementor-widget-text-editor" data-id="fde3730" data-element_type="widget" data-widget_type="text-editor.default"> <div class="elementor-widget-container"> <p>Founder, Principal</p> </div> </div> </div> </div> </div> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-0a837f7 e-flex e-con-boxed e-con e-parent nitro-offscreen" data-id="0a837f7" data-element_type="container" data-settings="{&quot;content_width&quot;:&quot;boxed&quot;}" data-core-v316-plus="true"> <div class="e-con-inner"> <div class="elementor-element elementor-element-b9e1b48
